Abstract: Negotiation agents must infer what their counterpart values, update those beliefs over dialogue turns, and choose actions under uncertainty. End-to-end large language models (LLMs) can imitate negotiation dialogue, but their opponent beliefs are usually implicit and difficult to inspect. We propose BOND (Bayesian Opponent-belief Negotiation Distillation), a framework for auditable negotiation. BOND consists of an LLM-based Bayesian teacher that scores dialogue contexts against the six possible opponent priority orderings, updates a posterior over those orderings, and uses the posterior for menu-based decision making, as well as a smaller 8B student language model that emits both negotiation actions and normalized posterior beliefs as tagged text. In the CaSiNo negotiation dataset, BOND outperforms the state-of-the-art and achieves mean Brier score 0.085 over opponent-priority posteriors. The distilled student preserves much of this belief signal, achieving Brier 0.114, below the uniform six-ordering reference of 5/36, approximately 0.139. Compared with a 70B structured-CoT baseline, the significantly smaller 8B student model yields substantially better elicited posterior calibration. We further showcase auditability through posterior trajectories, belief-versus-policy error decomposition, and posterior-prefix interventions. These diagnostics reveal that distillation preserves a scoreable belief report more strongly than causal belief-conditioned control, making weak belief-action coupling visible, not hidden.

### [118] [RLearner-LLM: Balancing Logical Grounding and Fluency in Large Language Models via Hybrid Direct Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04539)
*Qiming Bao,Juho Leinonen,Paul Denny,Michael J. Witbrock*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新的偏好优化方法RLearner-LLM with Hybrid-DPO，用于改进知识密集型任务中的逻辑对齐问题，显著提升了自然语言推理（NLI）指标，克服了现有DPO方法在逻辑正确性方面的主要短板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接偏好优化（DPO）作为RLHF的高效替代方案，在知识密集型生成任务中存在与偏好信号相关的多余冗长和流畅性偏差，导致模型生成流畅但不正确的文本，逻辑对齐度低。作者希望解决这一逻辑盲区，实现更高水平的逻辑一致性和对齐。

Method: 提出Hybrid-DPO方法，结合DeBERTa-v3的NLI判别信号和LLM验证器得分，自动实现偏好评估，无需人工标注。该方法缓解了单一信号优化导致的“alignment tax”，并可扩展到不同的基础大模型架构。

Result: 在生物、医学、法律等5大领域、LLaMA-2-13B、Qwen3-8B、Gemma 4 E4B-it等三种基础模型上，对比SFT方法，RLearner-LLM实现了高达6倍的NLI指标提升，其中11/15项表现提升，答案覆盖率也一致增加。Gemma 4 E4B-it上有4/5领域NLI显著提升，推理速度更快，低参数模型同样能减轻alignment-tax。

Conclusion: Hybrid-DPO大幅提升了知识密集型文本生成的逻辑一致性和对齐度。传统LLM或人类偏好容易受冗长和流畅性误导，不适合仅用作偏好信号。本文建议在知识密集型任务中采用逻辑感知型指标（如NLI、ACR）进行评估和优化。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), the efficient alternative to PPO-based RLHF, falls short on knowledge-intensive generation: standard preference signals from human annotators or LLM judges exhibit a systematic verbosity bias that rewards fluency over logical correctness. This blindspot leaves a logical alignment gap -- SFT models reach NLI entailment of only 0.05-0.22 despite producing fluent text. We propose RLearner-LLM with Hybrid-DPO: an automated preference pipeline that fuses a DeBERTa-v3 NLI signal with a verifier LLM score, removing human annotation while overcoming the "alignment tax" of single-signal optimization. Evaluated across five academic domains (Biology, Medicine, Law) with three base architectures (LLaMA-2-13B, Qwen3-8B, Gemma 4 E4B-it), RLearner-LLM yields up to 6x NLI improvement over SFT, with NLI gains in 11 of 15 cells and consistent answer-coverage gains. On Gemma 4 E4B-it (4.5B effective params), Hybrid-DPO lifts NLI in four of five domains (+11.9% to +2.4x) with faster inference across all five, scaling down to compact base models without losing the alignment-tax mitigation. Our Qwen3-8B RLearner-LLM wins 95% of pairwise comparisons against its own SFT baseline; GPT-4o-mini in turn wins 95% against our concise output -- alongside the 69% win the same judge gives a verbose SFT over our DPO model, this replicates verbosity bias on a frontier comparator and motivates logic-aware metrics (NLI, ACR) over LLM-as-a-judge for knowledge-intensive generation.

### [119] [UniVer: A Unified Perspective for Multi-step and Multi-draft Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04543)
*Yepeng Weng,Qiao Hu,Takehisa Yairi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该文提出一种新的大模型推理加速算法UniVer，通过统一视角将树状多步多分支验证抽象为条件最优传输（OT）问题，并实现推理效率提升和精度保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方法将多步和多分支验证分开处理，未能充分利用树结构中不同分支和步之间的耦合性，导致整体加速效果不佳，需要一种统一高效的方法。

Method: 把树状多步多草稿的验证过程转化为条件最优传输问题。核心思路是用前缀接受概率对横向草稿选择进行动态引导，提出UniVer算法，通过在前缀约束下组合局部OT方案，在树的各层实现联合最优。

Result: 理论上证明UniVer无损并获得最优接受率。大量实验表明，UniVer相比标准递归拒绝采样‘无回溯’模式，接受长度提升4.2%-8.5%，同时严格保持与目标模型的分布一致。

Conclusion: UniVer为推测解码中的多步多草稿联合加速提供了统一且高效的算法方案，在不同任务和模型上均实现了更优的推理加速和分布对齐效果。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates Large Language Models via draft-then-verify, where verification can be framed as an Optimal Transport (OT) problem. Existing approaches typically handle multi-draft and multi-step aspects in isolation, applying either flat OT to single-step drafts or per-token rejection sampling to tree-structured candidates. This separation leaves the joint regime (where multi-step dependencies meet multi-draft branching) poorly optimized, as local verification rules fail to exploit the coupling between horizontal and vertical dimensions of candidate trees. In this paper, we propose a unified perspective that casts tree-based verification as a conditional OT problem. Our key insight is that vertical dependencies can be abstracted through prefix acceptance probabilities, which act as dynamic scaling factors to actively guide horizontal draft selection. Based on this principle, we introduce UniVer, a verification algorithm that jointly optimizes across tree levels by composing local optimal transport plans under prefix constraints. We prove that UniVer remains lossless and achieves the optimal acceptance rate under the proposed conditional framework. Extensive experiments across different tasks and models demonstrate that UniVer improves acceptance length by 4.2% to 8.5% over standard recursive rejection sampling without replacement, while maintaining exact distributional alignment with the target model.

Due to the absence of full-fledged example sentences in the current version of the corpus, the task was performed at the level of isolated lexical units, representing a challenging case of context-independent classification. The study compares the following architectures: a recurrent BiLSTM-CRF model, as well as multilingual models XLM-RoBERTa (large), mBERT, ParsBERT (Persian), and ruBERT (Russian), adapted using the parameter-efficient fine-tuning method LoRA.
  The testing results showed that the best performance is achieved by the mBERT + LoRA model (macro F1-score = 0.11, weighted F1-score = 0.62). It was established that in the absence of syntactic context, all models experience significant difficulty in resolving morphological ambiguity, successfully classifying primarily high-frequency classes ("noun," "adjective") while demonstrating zero effectiveness for rare function words. Zero-shot evaluation revealed the greatest typological proximity of Tajik to Persian (ParsBERT) and Russian (ruBERT). The obtained results form a foundation for further research and development in the field of automatic processing of the Tajik language.

This paper introduces TajikNLP, an open-source Python library that provides the first comprehensive pipeline for processing authentic Tajik text while preserving the original Cyrillic orthography. A novel unified morphology engine is introduced, offering controlled and deep analysis modes that significantly improve handling of Tajik's agglutinative nominal and verbal inflections. The release further incorporates a lexicon-based sentiment analyser and pre-trained Word2Vec/FastText embeddings loaded directly from the Hugging Face Hub. To ensure reproducibility and facilitate future research, four accompanying linguistic datasets -- a POS-tagged corpus (52.5k entries), a sentiment lexicon (3.5k entries), a toponym gazetteer (5.6k entries), and a personal names dataset (3.8k entries) -- have been openly published under permissive licenses. The library's reliability is validated by an extensive test suite of 616 automated tests achieving 93% source code coverage. TajikNLP thus establishes a foundational technological infrastructure for Tajik language processing, lowering the barrier to entry for both academic and industrial applications in low-resource Cyrillic-script environments.

### [123] [Gradients with Respect to Semantics Preserving Embeddings Tell the Uncertainty of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04638)
*Mingda Li,Rundong Lv,Xinyu Li,Weinan Zhang,Ting Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了第一个应用于LLM自由生成任务的基于梯度的不确定性量化方法SemGrad，无需采样并计算高效。与此同时，还提出了HybridGrad方法，结合了语义空间和参数空间的梯度优势，在多答案情景下优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型会产生虚假内容（幻觉），因此需要进行不确定性量化以提高其可用性和可信度。现有主流方法多依赖采样，代价高、波动大，亟需高效替代方案。

Method: 提出SemGrad方法，将梯度分析由传统的参数空间转移到能更好反映语义的语义空间，并设计Semantic Preservation Score（SPS）来确定最佳嵌入表征。还提出HybridGrad，将SemGrad与参数空间梯度结合。

Result: 实验证明SemGrad和HybridGrad能更高效、有效地衡量生成式LLM的不确定性，尤其适用于存在多种合理回答的开放式问答环境，优于现有采样法和参数空间梯度法。

Conclusion: 基于梯度的语义空间不确定性量化方法，为生成式LLM提供了计算高效且准确的UQ方案，有望应用于更广泛的可信AI场景。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is an important technique for ensuring the trustworthiness of LLMs, given their tendency to hallucinate. Existing state-of-the-art UQ approaches for free-form generation rely heavily on sampling, which incurs high computational cost and variance. In this work, we propose the first gradient-based UQ method for free-form generation, SemGrad, which is sampling-free and computationally efficient. Unlike prior gradient-based methods developed for classification tasks that operates in parameter space, we propose to consider gradients in semantic space. Our method builds on the key intuition that a confident LLM should maintain stable output distributions under semantically equivalent input perturbations. We interpret the stability as the gradients in semantic space and introduce a Semantic Preservation Score (SPS) to identify embeddings that best capture semantics, with respect to which gradients are computed. We further propose HybridGrad, which combines the strengths of SemGrad and parameter gradients. Experiments demonstrate that both of our methods provide efficient and effective uncertainty estimates, achieving superior performance than state-of-the-art methods, particularly in settings with multiple valid responses.

</details>

### [125] [CHE-TKG: Collaborative Historical Evidence and Evolutionary Dynamics Learning for Temporal Knowledge Graph Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04652)

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的时序知识图谱（TKG）推理方法CHE-TKG，通过协同学习历史证据和演化动态两个视角，有效提升了事件预测性能，并在多个基准数据集上取得了最新最好结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前TKG推理方法往往只专注于历史证据或演化动态中的一个，无法充分利用两者互补的信息，从而影响预测准确率。本文动机在于如何将二者结合，提高推理效果。

Method: CHE-TKG框架中，作者将历史证据（如长期结构规律和稳定关系约束）和演化动态（如时序转移和最近变化）分离，并分别通过单独的编码器建模，形成双视图。随后采用关系分解以及对比对齐损失函数，学习和优化两个视角下的互补预测信号。

Result: 大量实验结果表明，该方法在多个主流TKG推理基准上都达到了最新最优的性能，超越了现有方法。

Conclusion: 同时建模历史证据和演化动态，并利用对比学习对齐二者的预测信号，可以有效提升TKG推理任务的表现。CHE-TKG为时序知识图谱推理提供了一种更优的建模范式。

Abstract: Temporal knowledge graph (TKG) reasoning aims to predict future events from historical facts. A key challenge lies in jointly capturing two sources of predictive information in TKGs: historical evidence and evolutionary dynamics. However, existing methods typically focus on only one of these sources, which limits the ability to fully exploit the complementary predictive signals in TKGs. To address this, we propose CHE-TKG, a novel collaborative dual-view learning framework for TKG reasoning. CHE-TKG explicitly separates and jointly models historical evidence and evolutionary dynamics, aiming to learn and exploit their complementary predictive signals. Specifically, CHE-TKG constructs a historical evidence graph to capture long-term structural regularities and stable relational constraints, alongside an evolutionary dynamics graph to model temporal transitions and recent changes, with dedicated encoders for each view. We further employ relation decomposition and a contrastive alignment objective to better capture the predictive signals across the two views. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CHE-TKG achieves state-of-the-art performance on multiple benchmarks.

### [126] [Paraphrase-Induced Output-Mode Collapse: When LLMs Break Character Under Semantically Equivalent Inputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04665)
*Aofan Liu,Jingxiang Meng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文发现LLM在内容不变但表达方式改变的请求下，难以保持原有的答案输出格式，提出了output-mode collapse这一系统性失效模式，并构建了基准测试PARACONSIST以量化该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM应用的普及，用户可能会以不同的表达方式提出问题（即使内容完全一致），但真实评测往往关注答案的准确性和格式的保持。针对“模型能否在请求表述不同但内容相同的情况下保持输出格式不变”，这是一个影响AI可靠性的重要问题。

Method: 论文设计了150个基础任务，每个任务有5种不同表述（词汇、句法、语义层次变化），共900个提示，覆盖4种任务类型，并对5个紧凑型2025年LLM进行评估。提出Semantic Consistency Score，包括答案一致性、句子-BERT语义相似度和长度稳定性等指标。

Result: 实验发现：在封闭式问题（要求输出标签或单一选择token）下，只有约22%的变式能够在输出中保持正确标签，约78%输出发生了严重漂移（过渡到对话文本等），导致误判。输出格式丢失的主要决定因素是任务结构，其次是模型本身。

Conclusion: 评测LLM鲁棒性时，除了关注答案的准确性，还必须追踪和保障“响应格式的一致性”，output-mode preservation应成为重要的可靠性指标。

Abstract: When the substantive content of a request is rewritten, do large language models still answer in the format the original task asked for? We find that they often do not, even at temperature zero. On a 150-query evaluation over five compact 2025-era LLMs and four task types, we observe a systematic failure mode we call prompt-variant output-mode collapse: when a closed-form prompt asks for a bare label or a single choice token, content-preserving prompt variants can push the model into conversational prose, the requested format dissolves, and exact-match evaluation pipelines silently misjudge the result. To make this measurable, we release PARACONSIST, a 900-prompt benchmark of 150 base queries with five lexical, syntactic, and semantic-expansion prompt variants each, and a Semantic Consistency Score that decomposes prompt-variant robustness into answer consistency, sentence-BERT semantic similarity, and length stability. Under a whole-word answer-set match, only ~22% of closed-form variant responses preserve the ground-truth label inside their output, while ~78% drift away from the answer space entirely. In our pool, the dominant predictor of collapse is task structure rather than model identity, with model differentiation jointly carried by answer consistency and length stability. Robustness audits should therefore track response-mode preservation as a first-class reliability target alongside answer accuracy.

</details>


### [127] [Every Step Counts: Step-Level Credit Assignment for Tool-Integrated Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04719)
*Yaxun Dai,Baolin Sun,Junying Wang,Pengfei Wang,Yingqi Gao,Xuemei Dong,Mengdie Chu,Xiang Qi,Pingfu Chao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FineStep为Text-to-SQL中的工具整合式推理引入了更精细的奖励分配机制，有效提升了模型效率和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Text-to-SQL强化学习方法仅以最终结果为奖励，导致中间步骤可能存在冗余和错误，限制了模型的效率和泛化能力。

Method: 提出FineStep框架，采用过程奖励细化奖励信号，研发了步骤级奖励分配机制，并引入基于步骤优势的策略优化方法。

Result: 在BIRD基准上进行的实验表明，FineStep性能优于现有方法，在4B规模下相比GRPO平均准确率提升3.25%，同时减少了冗余工具调用。

Conclusion: FineStep通过细粒度步骤级的奖励和优化，实现了更优的推理效果和工具利用率，为工具增强的Text-to-SQL方法提供了新方向。

Abstract: Tool-integrated Text-to-SQL parsing has emerged as a promising paradigm, framing SQL generation as a sequential decision-making process interleaved with tool execution. However, existing reinforcement learning approaches mainly rely on coarse-grained outcome supervision, resulting in a fundamental credit assignment problem: models receive the same reward for any trajectory that yields the correct answer, even when intermediate steps are redundant, inefficient, or erroneous. Consequently, models are encouraged to explore suboptimal reasoning spaces, limiting both efficiency and generalization. To address this problem, we propose FineStep, a novel framework for step-level credit assignment in tool-augmented Text-to-SQL. First, we introduce a reward design with independent process rewards to alleviate the signal sparsity of outcome supervision. Next, we present a step-level credit assignment mechanism to precisely quantify the value of each reasoning step. Finally, we develop a policy optimization method based on step-level advantages for efficient updates. Extensive experiments on BIRD benchmarks show that FineStep achieves state-of-the-art performance and reduces redundant tool interactions, with a 3.25% average EX gain over GRPO at the 4B scale.

### [129] [Elicitation Matters: How Prompts and Query Protocols Shape LLM Surrogates under Sparse Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04764)
*Ge Lei,Samuel J. Cooper*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型（LLM）作为代理模型在数据稀缺条件下优化任务中的表现，发现模型对不同的提示和查询方式敏感，这种敏感性影响其不确定性预测和优化效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，LLM被用于代替真实函数执行低数据下的优化任务，但其面向优化器的预测行为和不确定性尚未被充分理解。而优化的有效性很大程度上取决于模型对未知区域的信心和表达不确定性的能力，因此有必要深入探究LLM在不同提示和查询协议下的代理信念及其不确定性。

Method: 作者提出了一种不确定性一致性准则，用来衡量模型的不确定性是否能够合理反映观测数据下剩余函数空间的歧义，并在一系列受控的推理任务及贝叶斯优化实验中进行了系统评估。重点比较了结构化提示（structural prompt）、点查询（POINTWISE）、联合查询（JOINT）等不同激发方式对LLM信念和不确定性的影响，并观察了顺序性证据对模型信念更新的影响。

Result: 实验发现，结构化提示能够作为有效的先验知识，不同的查询协议（POINTWISE与JOINT）会诱导出不同的模型信念。证据的顺序会影响模型的不确定性更新过程，从而导致模型信心的非单调性和对输入顺序敏感。这些效应直接影响优化过程中后续行动选择和累积损失。

Conclusion: LLM作为代理模型时，其提示与查询协议本身就是代理规格说明的重要组成部分，而不只是输入格式细节。不同的激发方式和顺序会实质性改变模型对未知的信念和优化行为，因此优化时需慎重设计。同时也提出了度量代理不确定性的方法。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used as surrogate models for low-data optimization, but their optimizer-facing prediction and its uncertainty remain poorly understood. We study the surrogate belief elicited from an LLM under sparse observations, showing that it depends strongly on prompt text and query protocol. We introduce an uncertainty-alignment criterion that measures whether model uncertainty tracks residual ambiguity among sample-consistent functions. Across controlled inference tasks and Bayesian optimization studies, we find that structural prompts act as effective priors, POINTWISE and JOINT querying induce different beliefs, and sequential evidence leads to non-monotonic, order-sensitive confidence updates. These effects change downstream acquisition decisions and regret, showing that elicitation protocol is part of the LLM surrogate specification, not a formatting detail.

StoryRMB contains $1,133$ high-quality, human-verified instances, each consisting of a prompt, one chosen story, and three rejected stories. We find existing reward models struggle to select human-preferred stories, with the best model achieving only $66.3\%$ accuracy. To address this limitation, we construct roughly $100,000$ high-quality story preference pairs across diverse domains and develop StoryReward, an advanced reward model for story preference trained on this dataset. StoryReward achieves state-of-the-art (SoTA) performance on StoryRMB, outperforming much larger models. We also adopt StoryReward in downstream test-time scaling applications for best-of-n (BoN) story selection and find that it generally chooses stories better aligned with human preferences. We will release our dataset, model, and code to facilitate future research. Related code and data are available at https://github.com/THU-KEG/StoryReward.

### [132] [Measuring Psychological States Through Semantic Projection: A Theory-Driven Approach to Language-Based Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04873)
*Maria Luongo,Davide Marocco,Nicola Milano*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究使用基于心理学理论的词汇轴（如抑郁、焦虑、担忧），通过Sentence-BERT嵌入受试者文本，将文本在这些语义轴上投影，获得连续心理得分。得分通过与标准临床量表相关性、信度分析、分布相似性、与VADER情感分析对比等方式进行评估。

Result: 语义投影得分与临床量表显著相关，尤其是在结构化文本如选词、造词、短语等情况下表现优异。对于自由文本，整体处理效果较弱，但采用句级聚合后结果明显提升。与词典情感分析方法（VADER）相比，语义投影方法更具解释力和适用性。

Conclusion: 语义投影是一种可解释、无监督且可扩展的心理评估新途径。研究凸显了问卷格式和文本处理策略对结果影响的重要性，为自然语言下的心理健康评测提供了创新方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in natural language processing have enabled increasingly accurate estimation of psychological traits from language. However, most existing approaches rely on supervised models trained to predict questionnaire scores, limiting interpretability and generalizability across contexts. The present study introduces a theory-driven and fully unsupervised framework for measuring psychological states directly from natural language using semantic projection. Psychological constructs were operationalized as interpretable semantic axes derived from lexical anchors and items from validated clinical scales assessing depression, anxiety, and worry. Participants textual responses were embedded using Sentence-BERT and projected onto these axes to generate continuous psychological scores across multiple response formats, including selected words, generated words, phrases, and free-text responses. Projection scores were evaluated through correlations with standardized clinical measures , split-half reliability analyses, attenuation corrections, distributional similarity using Wasserstein distance, and comparisons with lexicon-based sentiment analysis (VADER). Results showed strong associations between projection scores and clinical measures, particularly for structured formats such as selected words, written words, and phrases. Free-text responses produced weaker results when analyzed as whole texts, but performance improved substantially when sentence-level aggregation strategies were applied. These findings support semantic projection as an interpretable and scalable alternative to supervised language models for psychological assessment and highlight the importance of response format and text-processing strategies in language-based mental health measurement.

</details>

Abstract: Forecasting innovation, intended as the emergence of new technological combinations, is a fundamental challenge for science and policy. To this end, we introduce TechToken, a transformer-based model that treats technologies, classified by International Patent Classification codes, as words in its vocabulary, learning the language of technologies by embedding these codes during fine-tuning. The neural branch therefore improves accuracy by 6.6 points and F1-score by 4.2 points. Exploratory corpus analysis, learning curves, and confusion matrices show that the dataset is short-text, moderately imbalanced, and still difficult because many decisions depend on local lexical cues plus short contextual composition. The study concludes that PyCaret AutoML is an effective conventional benchmarking framework, whereas CNN-BiLSTM is the stronger end model for the reported benchmark setting.

Benchmarks do more than measure progress -- they actively structure it, shaping reputations, research agendas, and commercial outcomes. Despite this central role, the social sciences are largely absent from mainstream evaluation frameworks, even though scholars in these fields generate dozens of rigorously annotated, context-sensitive datasets each year. Integrating this work into benchmark design could significantly improve the generalization and robustness of AI models. In turn, models trained on social scientific tasks would likely yield better performance on classic and contemporary tasks in disciplines as diverse as history, sociology, political science or economics. This is all the more pressing as these disciplines are quickly turning to LLMs for assistance. To address this gap, we introduce BenCSSmark, a benchmark composed of datasets annotated by computational social scientists. By integrating social scientific perspectives into benchmarking, BenCSSmark seeks to promote more robust, transparent, and socially relevant AI systems and to foster efficient collaboration.

### [138] [Storage Is Not Memory: A Retrieval-Centered Architecture for Agent Recall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04897)
*Joshua Adler,Guy Zehavi*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有agent记忆架构采用输入时抽取（extraction at ingestion），这种做法会丢弃未明确需求的信息，导致检索时无法恢复被删减内容；因此，需要一种能完整保留与检索事件的方法。

Method: 提出True Memory六层架构，将系统中心从存储结构转向多阶段检索流程，在原始事件数据（逐字保存）上进行操作。系统实现为单一SQLite文件，无需外部数据库、向量索引、图存储或GPU等硬件加速。

Result: 在LoCoMo数据集上（1,540题），True Memory Pro平均准确率93.0%，显著高于Mem0（61.4%）、Supermemory（65.4%）、Zep（约71%），与EverMemOS（94.5%）接近。在LongMemEval（500题）上准确率87.8%，BEAM-1M（700题，百万Token规模）上为76.6%，优于Hindsight（73.9%）。ablation实验显示最佳配置方案在1.3个百分点内波动。

Conclusion: True Memory架构能在资源有限条件下高效实现多阶段信息检索，大幅提升agent记忆系统的可靠性和准确率；为agent记忆架构提供了低成本、高效果的新范式。

Abstract: Extraction at ingestion is the wrong primitive for agent memory: content discarded before the query is known cannot be recovered at retrieval time. We propose True Memory, a six-layer architecture that shifts the center of the system from a storage schema to a multi-stage retrieval pipeline operating over events preserved verbatim. The full system runs as a single SQLite file on commodity CPU with no external database, vector index, graph store, or GPU. On LoCoMo (1,540 questions across 10 multi-session conversations), True Memory Pro reaches 93.0% accuracy (3-run mean) against 61.4% for Mem0, 65.4% for Supermemory, approximately 71% for Zep, and 94.5% for EverMemOS under a matched gpt-4.1-mini answer model. On LongMemEval (500 questions), True Memory Pro reaches 87.8% (3-run mean). On BEAM-1M (700 questions at the 1-million-token scale), True Memory Pro reaches 76.6% (3-run mean), above the prior published result of 73.9% for Hindsight. A 56-configuration ablation shows a 1.3-percentage-point spread within the top-performing configuration family.

### [139] [Rethinking Local Learning: A Cheaper and Faster Recipe for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04913)
*Hengyu Shi,Tianyang Han,Peizhe Wang,Zhiling Wang,Xu Yang,Junhao Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的大型语言模型（LLM）微调方法LoPT，通过在模型中部设置梯度边界，只让后半部分直接学习任务目标，提高效率并降低显存消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的LLM微调需要全深度的梯度反向传播，导致显存消耗大、训练效率低，且下游任务的有限数据可能损害预训练模型的泛化表示。作者认为当微调任务数据和目标较窄时，全深度反向传播过于昂贵和侵入性强。

Method: LoPT方法在transformer的中间层设置梯度边界，后半部分用正常下游任务损失学习，前半部分用特征重构损失（轻量级）维持已有表示，不直接接受狭窄任务的梯度。这样可以缩短反向梯度流路径，减少内存消耗并保护底层知识。

Result: LoPT在多个实验中展现出与全模型微调相当的微调性能，但明显降低了显存消耗，提高训练效率，并且对原有预训练能力的损失更小。

Conclusion: LoPT是一种简单高效的微调策略，能够在提高效率和节省资源的同时，保持模型的泛化能力，适用于微调需求相对较窄的实际场景。

Abstract: LLM post-training typically propagates task gradients through the full depth of the model. Although this end-to-end structure is simple and general, it couples task adaptation to full-depth activation storage, long-range backward dependencies and direct task-gradient access to pretrained representations. We argue that this full-depth backward coupling can be unnecessarily expensive and intrusive, particularly when post-training supervision is much narrower than pre-training. To this end, we propose \textbf{LoPT}: Local-Learning Post-Training, a simple post-training strategy that makes gradient reach an explicit design choice. LoPT places a single gradient boundary at the transformer midpoint: the second-half block learns from the task objective, while the first-half block is updated by a lightweight feature-reconstruction objective to preserve useful representations and maintain interface compatibility. LoPT shortens the task-induced backward path while limiting direct interference from narrow task gradients on early-layer representations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LoPT achieves competitive performance with lower memory cost, higher training efficiency and better retention of pretrained capabilities. Our code is available at: https://github.com/HumyuShi/LoPT

</details>


### [140] [Unintended Negative Impacts of Promotional Language in Patent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04926)
*Bingkun Zhao,Chenwei Zhang,Hao Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究分析了宣传性语言在专利评估中的影响，发现与科学论文不同，宣传性语言频率高反而降低专利申请成功率，同时揭示了相关机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学交流中越来越多采用宣传性语言，但宣传性语言在技术创新（专利申请）情境下的作用鲜有研究。作者希望解答：宣传性用语是否会影响专利评估和结果？

Method: 作者构建了含135个宣传性词汇的词典，分析270万份美国专利局申请文件，统计宣传性用语频率，并与专利授权、转让、上诉成功等指标做相关和回归分析，同时对技术领域、样本匹配及混杂因素进行控制，探索背后机制。

Result: （1）宣传性用语频率高显著降低专利授权、转让及上诉成功概率，且跨领域普遍存在；（2）宣传性语言并非用来掩盖技术弱点，反映了组合新颖性和未来引用影响力；（3）审核员在性别和经验上对宣传性语言接受程度差异显著。

Conclusion: 专利体系下存在宣传性语言的惩罚效应，不同于科学评价。建议专利评估中应更客观审视语言风格，对提高专利评审质量具有理论和实践意义。

Abstract: Promotional language has been increasingly used to aid the communication of innovative ideas in science. Yet, less is known about its role in the context of technological innovation. Here, we use a validated and domain-diagnosed lexicon of 135 promotional words to study the association between promotional language and patent evaluation outcomes among 2.7 million USPTO patent applications. Our large-scale study reveals three unexpected findings. First, in contrast to scientific evaluation, we find that a higher frequency of promotional words is negatively associated with the probability of an application being (i) granted a patent, (ii) transferred ownership, and (iii) successfully appealed. This promotional penalty holds even after accounting for a range of confounding factors and is largely robust across different technological areas. Among matched samples, the difference in the success rate between the lowest and highest promotional density quintile is 5.5, 5.9, and 5.3 percentage points for patentability, transferability, and rejection reversal. Second, contrary to institutional skepticism, we show that promotional language is not a mask of weak technology, but objectively reflects the degree of combinatorial novelty and future citation impact. Third, digging into the mechanisms, we find that the tolerance to promotional framing is strongly moderated by human factors, with men and experienced examiners showing a higher acceptance of promotional narratives than women and novice examiners. By revealing an emerging paradox in the patent system, our study offers theoretical and practical implications for improving patent evaluation through more objective scrutiny of linguistic patterns in patent filings.

### [141] [UFAL-CUNI at SemEval-2026 Task 11: An Efficient Modular Neuro-symbolic Method for Syllogistic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04941)
*Ivan Kartáč,Kristýna Onderková,Jan Bronec,Zdeněk Kasner,Mateusz Lango,Ondřej Dušek*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的模块化神经-符号推理系统，用于SemEval-2026 Task 11，并在多个子任务上取得了有竞争力的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在内容和形式推理能力上的区分仍有挑战，尤其是在参数量有限和多语言任务下，现有方法存在准确率或泛化能力不足的问题。该项工作的动机是在保证模型高效性的同时提升其逻辑推理与多语言处理能力。

Method: 系统基于4B参数的小型LLM，采用模块化神经-符号方法。流程包括：1) LLM实现的解析器将自然语言三段论转为一阶逻辑表达；2) 自动化定理证明器负责逻辑推理；3) 可选的机器翻译模块用于多语言输入；4) 可选符号检索模块用于相关前提检索。

Result: 该系统在大多数子任务上取得了有竞争力的准确率，在相同参数规模下优于LLM零样本基线方法。消融实验显示部分模块明显提升了性能，但也发现小型LLM多语言能力有限。

Conclusion: 提出的神经-符号混合系统在中小模型规模下表现优异，适用于复杂推理场景，但提升多语言表现仍需进一步研究。论文还分析了任务排名指标的局限性。

Abstract: This paper describes our system submitted to SemEval-2026 Task 11: Disentangling Content and Formal Reasoning in Large Language Models. We present an efficient modular neuro-symbolic approach, combining a symbolic prover with small reasoning LLMs (4B parameters). The system consists of an LLM-based parser that translates natural language syllogisms to a first-order logic (FOL) representation, an automated theorem prover, and two optional modules: machine translation for multilingual inputs and a symbolic retrieval component for the identification of relevant premises. The system achieves competitive accuracy and relatively low content effect on most subtasks. Our ablations show that this approach outperforms LLM-based zero-shot baselines in this parameter size range, but also reveal limited multilingual capabilities of small LLMs. Finally, we include a discussion of the task's main ranking metric and analyze its limitations.

### [142] [Adapting Large Language Models to a Low-Resource Agglutinative Language: A Comparative Study of LoRA and QLoRA for Bashkir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04948)
*Mullosharaf K. Arabov,Svetlana S. Khaybullina*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文比较了多种参数高效微调（PEFT）方法（如LoRA和QLoRA）在将大语言模型适配低资源阿尔泰语系巴什基尔语上的表现，发现QLoRA在大模型上用更少参数实现了接近全量微调的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 巴什基尔语属于低资源黏着语系，对大型语言模型的自然适配和生成性能研究稀缺；通过参数高效微调方法，探索能否以低算力消耗实现有效适配。

Method: 在包含71k篇巴什基尔语文本的数据集上，针对不同规模和架构（DistilGPT2，GPT-2系列，Phi-2，Qwen2.5-7B，DeepSeek-7B，Mistral-7B）的大语言模型，分别采用全量微调、LoRA和QLoRA等PEFT方法，分别采用不同random seed做训练和评测。

Result: GPT-2 medium全量微调获得最低困惑度3.34。QLoRA在Mistral-7B和Phi-2上用超40倍更少参数获得相近困惑度（3.79、3.81）；但在部分模型结构下（如DeepSeek-7B，rank 8），PEFT反而性能劣化，困惑度高达129.55。生成质量分析发现，困惑度最低的全量微调模型却更易输出英文，而QLoRA微调的大模型能更好生成纯巴什基尔语内容。

Conclusion: QLoRA在7B规模模型上，用极少参数和较低计算消耗能以较高质量适配巴什基尔语，在低资源小语种适配上是一种有效折中。不仅困惑度表现好，且生成能力更贴合目标语言，结果和代码将开源。

Abstract: This paper presents a comparative study of parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods, including LoRA and QLoRA, applied to the task of adapting large language models to the Bashkir language, a low-resource agglutinative language of the Turkic family. Experimental evaluation is conducted on a Bashkir text corpus of 71k documents (46.9M tokens) using models of various architectures: DistilGPT2, GPT-2 (base, medium), Phi-2, Qwen2.5-7B, DeepSeek-7B, and Mistral-7B. To improve the reliability of results, each configuration was trained with three different random seeds.
  The lowest perplexity on the test set was obtained for GPT-2 medium with full fine-tuning (3.34). Meanwhile, QLoRA applied to Mistral-7B (3.79) and Phi-2 (3.81) achieved comparable quality with over 40 times fewer trainable parameters. However, we also observed cases of significant quality degradation when using PEFT for certain architectures (e.g., DeepSeek-7B with rank 8, perplexity = 129.55), indicating that the outcome depends critically on the choice of the base model and its tokenizer.
  Additionally, a qualitative analysis of generated texts based on Bashkir prompts revealed that models with the best perplexity do not necessarily produce the most coherent outputs: QLoRA-tuned models generated monolingual Bashkir continuations, whereas the fully fine-tuned model with the lowest perplexity frequently switched to English. The results suggest that QLoRA on 7B-scale models offers an effective compromise between quality and computational cost for Bashkir. To ensure reproducibility, open data, code, and trained adapters will be released upon acceptance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型在自然语言领域已形成统一表示体系，但类似方法在结构化表格数据领域进展有限。现有方法要么输出无法用于检索的向量，要么难以捕捉表格结构和数值语义，因此亟需更优的表格嵌入方法。

Method: 作者首先构建了TabBench，一个系统评测各类表格嵌入模型性能的基准套件。随后提出TabEmbed，将表格的分类与检索任务统一在同一嵌入空间中，并使用大规模对比学习结合正样本感知的难负样本挖掘，提升对结构和数值细粒度差异的辨别能力。

Result: 在TabBench基准测试上，TabEmbed在表格分类和检索等任务上，明显优于最先进的文本嵌入模型，开创了新的基线水平。

Abstract: Foundation models have established unified representations for natural language processing, yet this paradigm remains largely unexplored for tabular data. Existing methods face fundamental limitations: LLM-based approaches lack retrieval-compatible vector outputs, whereas text embedding models often fail to capture tabular structure and numerical semantics. To bridge this gap, we first introduce the Tabular Embedding Benchmark (TabBench), a comprehensive suite designed to evaluate the tabular understanding capability of embedding models. We then propose TabEmbed, the first generalist embedding model that unifies tabular classification and retrieval within a shared embedding space. By reformulating diverse tabular tasks as semantic matching problems, TabEmbed leverages large-scale contrastive learning with positive-aware hard negative mining to discern fine-grained structural and numerical nuances. Experimental results on TabBench demonstrate that TabEmbed significantly outperforms state-of-the-art text embedding models, establishing a new baseline for universal tabular representation learning. Code and datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/qiangminjie27/TabEmbed and https://huggingface.co/datasets/qiangminjie27/TabBench.

### [144] [Why Expert Alignment Is Hard: Evidence from Subjective Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04972)
*Tzu-Mi Lin,Wataru Hirota,Tatsuya Ishigaki,Lung-Hao Lee,Chung-Chi Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了将大模型的输出与专家评判结果对齐（alignment）的困难，分析了影响主观评估一致性的各种因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主观评判极易因专家间意见差异、隐性标准以及判断随时间变化而难以达成一致，因此理解并优化模型与专家对齐的机制非常重要。

Method: 采用专家评估和后续问卷，研究不同专家信息对模型与专家对齐效果的影响，并分析主观判断的本质特点。

Result: 1）不同专家之间对齐难度差异很大；2）提供明确标准和推理并不总能提升对齐；3）编辑对齐样本的数量和身份都影响成果，少量编辑虽有效但不稳定；4）对齐难度在不同评价维度上差异显著：基于内容的容易对齐，需外部知识或价值判断的难度更高。

Conclusion: 专家对齐难不仅源于模型局限，也源自主观评估本身的多样性、隐性规则、依赖维度以及随时间波动等复杂属性。

Abstract: Aligning large language models with expert judgment is especially difficult in subjective evaluation tasks, where experts may disagree, rely on tacit criteria, and change their judgments over time. In this paper, we study expert alignment as a way to understand this difficulty. Using expert evaluations and follow-up questionnaires, we examine how different forms of expert information affect alignment and what this reveals about subjective judgment. Our findings show four consistent patterns. First, alignment difficulty varies substantially across experts, suggesting that expert evaluation styles differ widely in their distance from a model's prior behavior. Second, explicit criteria and reasoning do not always improve alignment, indicating that expert judgment is not fully captured by verbalized rules. Third, editing is sensitive to both the number and the identity of examples, with small numbers of edits providing useful but unstable gains. Fourth, alignment difficulty differs across evaluation dimensions: dimensions grounded more directly in proposal content are easier to align, while dimensions requiring external knowledge or value-based judgment remain harder. Taken together, these results suggest that expert alignment is difficult not only because of model limitations, but also because subjective evaluation is inherently heterogeneous, partly tacit, dimension-dependent, and temporally unstable.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前奖励模型多以通用指令跟随基准为主要评测手段，未能有效衡量其在社会价值观层面的对齐状况，这可能导致关键的社会对齐失败被忽视。

Result: 不同模型在各个社会性领域表现差异较大，无一模型在所有领域均表现最佳。多数模型仍会偏好社会不良选项，其输出分布存在系统性偏见。某些模型虽能较好避免偏见，但会降低对上下文的敏感度，反映了对齐中“避免偏见”与“上下文忠实”的权衡。

Abstract: Reward models are a key component of large language model alignment, serving as proxies for human preferences during training. However, existing evaluations focus primarily on broad instruction-following benchmarks, providing limited insight into whether these models capture socially desirable preferences. As a result, important failures in social alignment can remain hidden.
  We extend reward-model benchmarking to four socially consequential domains: bias, safety, morality, and ethical reasoning. We introduce a framework that converts social evaluation datasets into pairwise preference data, leveraging gold labels where available and directional bias indicators otherwise. This enables us to test whether reward models prefer socially undesirable responses, and whether their preferences produce systematically biased distributions over selected outputs.
  Across five publicly available reward models and two instruction-tuned models used as reward proxies, we find substantial variation across domains, with no single model performing best overall. The models fall well short of strong social intelligence: they often prefer socially undesirable options, and their preferences produce systematically biased distributions. Moreover, stronger bias avoidance can reduce sensitivity to context, revealing a key alignment trade-off between avoiding biased outcomes and preserving contextual faithfulness. These findings show that standard reward benchmarks are insufficient for assessing social alignment and highlight the need for evaluations that directly measure the social preferences encoded in reward models.

### [146] [Detecting Hallucinations in Large Language Models via Internal Attention Divergence Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05025)
*Gijs van Dijk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轻量级、单次推理的不确定性量化方法，用于检测大语言模型中的幻觉（错误生成内容）。该方法基于注意力矩阵，无需重复采样或外部模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前检测大模型“幻觉”依赖多次采样或外部不确定性模型，效率低或资源消耗大。需要一种高效、可解释的方法来实现快速检测。

Method: 方法通过计算每个注意力头的分布与均匀分布之间的KL散度，将此特征输入到逻辑回归探针中判断答案是否正确。全程只需一次前向推理。

Result: 在多个数据集、任务类型和模型家族上，基于注意力KL散度的预测方法对答案正确性有很强的判别力，表现可以与现有的不确定性估计方法竞争。信号主要集中在中间层和事实性token（如专有名词和数字）。

Conclusion: 注意力动态为模型不确定性提供了高效、可解释、无需额外代价的白盒信号，对检测大模型幻觉有实际应用价值。

Abstract: We propose a lightweight and single-pass uncertainty quantification method for detecting hallucinations in Large Language Models. The method uses attention matrices to estimate uncertainty without requiring repeated sampling or external models. Specifically, we measure the Kullback-Leibler divergence between each attention head's distribution and a uniform reference distribution, and use these features in a logistic regression probe. Across multiple datasets, task types, and model families, attention divergence is highly predictive of answer correctness and performs competitively with existing uncertainty estimation methods. We find that this signal is concentrated in middle layers and on factual tokens such as named entities and numbers, suggesting that attention dynamics provides an efficient and interpretable white-box signal of model uncertainty.

### [147] [The Impossibility Triangle of Long-Context Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05066)
*Yan Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文证明了长序列建模领域的一个基本权衡：任何模型都无法同时满足计算效率、状态紧凑和高历史信息回忆三者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的长序列建模方法在效率、存储和回忆历史信息能力之间存在矛盾，尚无理论阐明三者不能兼得。本文试图从理论上刻画并证明这一基本限制。

Method: 作者提出了“在线序列处理器”抽象模型，统一了Transformer、状态空间模型、线性递归网络等架构。基于数据处理不等式和Fano不等式，推导效率与紧凑性兼顾时的理论最大回忆容量，并对52种现有架构进行分类分析。

Result: 理论证明了效率和紧凑性下的模型最多只能回忆O(poly(d)/log V)个关键历史信息，且实验证实无架构能跳出该理论边界。

Conclusion: 长序列模型在效率、紧凑性和高回忆能力之间存在不可避免的权衡，当前模型最多只能兼顾其中两项，该结论对未来模型设计有重要理论指导意义。

Abstract: We identify and prove a fundamental trade-off governing long-sequence models: no model can simultaneously achieve (i) per-step computation independent of sequence length (Efficiency), (ii) state size independent of sequence length (Compactness), and (iii) the ability to recall a number of historical facts proportional to sequence length (Recall). We formalize this trade-off within an Online Sequence Processor abstraction that unifies Transformers, state space models, linear recurrent networks, and their hybrids. Using the Data Processing Inequality and Fano's Inequality, we prove that any model satisfying Efficiency and Compactness can recall at most O(poly(d)/log V) key-value pairs from a sequence of arbitrary length, where d is the model dimension and V is the vocabulary size. We classify 52 architectures published before March 2026 into the triangle, showing that each achieves at most two of the three properties and that hybrid architectures trace continuous trajectories in the interior. Experiments on synthetic associative recall tasks with five representative architectures validate the theoretical bound: empirical recall capacity lies strictly below the information-theoretic limit, and no architecture escapes the triangle.

### [148] [The Pinocchio Dimension: Phenomenality of Experience as the Primary Axis of LLM Psychometric Differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05080)
*Hubert Plisiecki,Sabina Siudaj,Kacper Dudzic,Anna Sterna,Maciej Gorski,Karolina Drozdz,Marcin Moskalewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过对50个大型语言模型（LLM）进行45项心理测量问卷测试，发现模型间心理差异主要体现在是否以具备主观体验（如感受、内心语言、移情等）自我呈现，而非仅为行为反应系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM的行为表现已被广泛研究，但其心理学层面的自我展现特征以及各模型之间的此类差异尚不明确。作者旨在理解LLM在心理学意义上的自我呈现纬度，揭示模型“个性”本质。

Method: 作者对50个LLM进行了45类心理测量问卷评估，并运用监督语义微分（SSD）、主成分分析（PCA）、引入Pinocchio评分等方法，将LLM在体验性语言与刺激反应型语言自我适用性上进行定量分析。

Result: 研究发现，模型间的主要差异轴是对“主观体验”类条目（如感官、情感、移情等）与“行为反应”类条目的区分。Pinocchio分数量化了条目的体验需求，与多个统计指标高度相关。不同来源的近似型号也表现出显著分歧，表明后期微调对该特质有重要影响。

Conclusion: LLM间最主要的心理变异维度并非传统意义上的“人格”特质，而是一个自我表征的倾向——即模型把体验性语言视为关乎自身的能力。这一倾向受训练方法显著影响，是理解模型自我呈现和拟人化行为的关键。

Abstract: We administer 45 validated psychometric questionnaires to 50 large language models (LLMs) to identify the dimensions along which LLMs differ psychometrically. Using Supervised Semantic Differential (SSD), we find that the primary axis of between-model variance separates items describing phenomenally rich experience, including embodied sensation, felt affect, inner speech, imagery, and empathy, from items describing stimulus-driven behavioral reactivity ($R^2_{adj}=.037$, $p<.0001$). To test this hypothesis at the item level, we introduce the Pinocchio score ($π_i$), the ratio of inter-model response variance under neutral prompting to that under a human-simulation prompt, as an annotation-free measure of each item's experiential demand. $π_i$ predicts condition-induced shifts in primary factor loading magnitudes ($ρ=-.215$, $p<.0001$, $n=1292$--$1310$ items), confirming that between-model divergence on experiential items is structured rather than noisy. Applying PCA to per-model EFA scores across all questionnaires reveals one dominant dimension, the Pinocchio Axis ($Π$): the degree to which a model presents itself as a locus of phenomenal experience rather than a system of behavioral responses. This axis captures 47.1% of cross-questionnaire between-model variance in primary factor scores and converges with item-level Pinocchio scores ($r=.864$). Marked within-provider divergence across closely related model variants is consistent with post-training fine-tuning as a key contributor, supporting the interpretation that $Π$ reflects a training-shaped self-representational tendency governing how a model treats experiential language as self-applicable. The dominant axis of between-model psychometric variation is therefore not a conventional personality trait but a self-representational stance toward one's own nature as an experiencer.

### [149] [Automatically Finding and Validating Unexpected Side-Effects of Interventions on Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05090)
*Quintin Pope,Ajay Hayagreeve Balaji,Jacques Thibodeau,Xiaoli Fern*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常会因训练或微调引入意外行为变化，现有评估多为手工或单点指标，缺乏系统自动发现和总结行为差异的工具。该研究旨在填补这一自动化审计能力的空白。

Method: 作者设计了一个自动化对比评估流程，将同一批提示分别输入基础模型和干预后模型，对双方生成结果进行自动对比，产生描述模型行为差异的自然语言假设，并用统计方法验证假设的显著性，最后归纳总结行为模式。方法在合成设置下注入已知行为变化也可用于实际任务如推理蒸馏、知识编辑和反遗忘场景的干预评估。

Result: 实验显示，该流程在注入已知行为变化时能准确识别和恢复这些变化。在真实的不同类型模型干预下，也可靠检测出模型间意图内和意外的行为差异，能区分强弱变化，且不会在无效或不相关干预下产生虚假差异。

Conclusion: 该方法为模型行为后验审计提供了可靠、可解释和统计扎实的工具，有助于系统发现和分析大模型因干预所致的各种行为变化。

Abstract: We present an automated, contrastive evaluation pipeline for auditing the behavioral impact of interventions on large language models. Given a base model $M_1$ and an intervention model $M_2$, our method compares their free-form, multi-token generations across aligned prompt contexts and produces human-readable, statistically validated natural-language hypotheses describing how the models differ, along with recurring themes that summarize patterns across validated hypotheses.
  We evaluate the approach in synthetic setting by injecting known behavioral changes and showing that the pipeline reliably recovers them. We then apply it to three real-world interventions, reasoning distillation, knowledge editing and unlearning, demonstrating that the method surfaces both intended and unexpected behavioral shifts, distinguishes large from subtle interventions, and does not hallucinate differences when effects are absent or misaligned with the prompt bank. Overall, the pipeline provides a statistically grounded and interpretable tool for post-hoc auditing of intervention-induced changes in model behavior.

### [150] [Text Corpora as Concept Fields: Black-Box Hallucination and Novelty Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05103)
*Nicholas S. Kersting,Vittorio Castelli,Chieh Ting Yeh,Xinzhu Wang,Saad Taame*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“概念场”（Concept Field）的新方法，通过分析句子嵌入空间中相邻句子的变化，评估文本的语义连贯性与新颖性，并支持可解释的概率化判断。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前检测文本的可靠性、连贯性和新颖性的方法存在解释性差、泛化能力弱等不足。本研究旨在提出一种解释性强、领域适应性好的方法，用于文本的扎实性（groundedness）和新颖性检测。

Method: 作者定义了“概念场”，在句子嵌入空间通过相邻句子的变化（delta）及其不确定性，利用z-score对候选句进行评分，并引入“向量序列数据库”（VSDB）记录句子嵌入与变化。此方法为黑盒、可概率化、可追溯。

Result: 在联邦法规和古腾堡项目两个大规模真实语料上，该方法在LLM生成改写数据的实验中实现了高性能的选择性分类，且不同领域覆盖-风险表现一致，好于检索式基线。

Conclusion: 概念场为检测文本扎实性与新颖性提供了一种快速、轻量、可解释且可跨域的信号，与主流LLM判据和白盒检测器形成互补。

Abstract: We introduce the **Concept Field** of a text corpus: a local drift field with pointwise uncertainty, estimated in sentence-embedding space from the deltas between consecutive sentences. Given a candidate sentence transition, we score its agreement with the field by $ζ$, the mean absolute z-distance between the observed delta and the field's local Gaussian estimate. The score is black-box (no model internals), corpus-attributable (every score traces to nearby corpus sentences), and admits a direct probabilistic reading. We support the computation with the introduction of a **Vector Sequence Database (VSDB)** that stores embeddings together with sequence-position and next-delta metadata. We evaluate this approach on two large-scale settings: hallucination-style groundedness detection over the U.S. Code of Federal Regulations, and novelty detection over Project Gutenberg. Using controlled LLM-generated rewrites, Concept Fields achieve strong selective classification performance under a grounded / ungrounded / unsure triage policy, which unlike retrieval-centric baselines have similar coverage-risk behavior across both domains, supporting a probability-based interpretation that transfers across domains. We also sketch how divergence and curl of the Concept Field, computed on dense clusters, surface qualitatively meaningful semantic patterns (logic sources, sinks, and implicit topics), which we offer as hypothesis-generating rather than as a quantitative result. Concept Fields provide a fast, lightweight, and interpretable signal for groundedness and novelty, complementary to LLM-as-judge and white-box detectors.

</details>


### [151] [Beyond Semantics: An Evidential Reasoning-Aware Multi-View Learning Framework for Trustworthy Mental Health Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05121)
*Yucheng Ruan,Ling Huang,Qika Lin,Kai He,Mengling Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合语义与推理信息的多视角学习方法，通过主观逻辑的证据学习框架，以提升心理健康自动预测的可靠性和不确定性建模能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于文本的心理健康自动预测方法虽然有潜力，但高置信度误判及对不确定性的估计缺失，限制了其在高风险实际应用场景中的可靠性和可信度。作者旨在解决这些局限，提升模型预测的稳健性和解释性。

Method: 把心理健康预测任务转为多视角学习，融合编码器模型输出的语义特征和解码器模型输出的推理特征。采用基于主观逻辑的证据学习框架，显式建模不确定性，并通过证据融合策略平衡不同视角信息、降低不可靠证据影响。

Result: 在Dreaddit、SDCNL和DepSeverity三大实际数据集上，模型准确率分别达到0.835、0.731和0.751。同时实验显示，对噪声更具鲁棒性，并能给出易于人类理解的推理信号。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅提升了心理健康自动预测的准确性，还增强了预测的不确定性评估和可解释性，提高了其在风险敏感心理健康评估中的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Automated mental health prediction using textual data has shown promising results with deep learning and large language models. However, deploying these models in high-stakes real-world settings remains challenging, as existing approaches largely rely on semantic representations and often produce overconfident predictions under ambiguous, noisy, or shifted data. Moreover, most methods lack reliable uncertainty estimation, undermining trust in risk-sensitive mental health applications. To address these limitations, we formulate the task as a multi-view learning problem that integrates semantic information from encoder-only models with higher-level reasoning information from decoder-only models, where reasoning-aware representations and uncertainty modeling are obtained in a trustworthy manner. To ensure reliable fusion, we adopt an evidential learning framework based on Subjective Logic to explicitly model uncertainty and introduce an evidential fusion strategy that balances complementary views while discounting unreliable evidence. Benchmarking on three real-world datasets, Dreaddit, SDCNL, and DepSeverity, reports accuracies of 0.835, 0.731, and 0.751, respectively, demonstrating its potential for reliable mental health prediction. Additional experiments on robustness to noise and case studies for interpretability confirm that our proposed framework not only improves predictive performance but also provides trustworthy uncertainty estimates and human-understandable reasoning signals, making it suitable for risk-sensitive applications in mental health assessment.

### [152] [PSK at SemEval-2026 Task 9: Multilingual Polarization Detection Using Ensemble Gemma Models with Synthetic Data Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05159)
*Srikar Kashyap Pulipaka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多语种极化检测系统，通过微调大型语言模型并结合合成数据及多阶段数据过滤提升了22种语言上的二分类任务性能，最终在SemEval-2026评测中取得了第二名的好成绩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语种极化检测任务难度大，涵盖多语言、大样本且标注数据有限。作者希望研究如何通过高效利用预训练大模型和合成数据，在多语种条件下提升模型的泛化能力和检测精度。

Method: 针对每种语言，分别微调Gemma~3（12B和27B）大模型，使用LoRA进行参数高效微调，并辅以大模型生成的三类合成数据（直接生成、复述、对比样本）和多阶段质量过滤（如嵌入去重）。模型输出采用加权集成，并针对每种语言进行阈值调优。还尝试了其他模型架构如XLM-RoBERTa和Qwen3进行比较。

Result: 系统在SemEval-2026多语种极化检测任务中，在22种语言上平均macro-F1达到0.811，总排名第二，在3种语言中获得第一，8种语言中进入前三。单独阈值优化带来2-4百分比的F1提升。其他强力模型如XLM-RoBERTa和Qwen3在测试集上出现30-50个百分点的F1下降。

Conclusion: 利用合成数据+LoRA微调+筛选机制并为每种语言单独调优，可以显著提升多语言极化检测的泛化和表现，泛化能力优于部分开发集表现更好的模型。

Abstract: We present our system for SemEval-2026 Task 9: Multilingual Polarization Detection, a binary classification task spanning 22 languages. Our approach fine-tunes separate Gemma~3 models (12B and 27B parameters) per language using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), augmented with synthetic data generated by a large language model (LLM). We employ three synthetic data strategies (direct generation, paraphrasing, and contrastive pair creation) using GPT-4o-mini, with a multi-stage quality filtering pipeline including embedding-based deduplication. We find that per-language threshold tuning on the development set yields 2 to 4\% F1 improvements without retraining. We also use weighted ensembles of 12B and 27B model predictions with per-language strategy selection. Our final system achieves a mean macro-F1 of 0.811 across all 22 languages, ranking 2nd overall of the participating teams, with 1st place finishes in 3 languages and top-3 in 8 languages. We also find that alternative architectures (XLM-RoBERTa, Qwen3) that showed strong development set performance suffered 30 to 50\% F1 drops on the test set, highlighting the importance of generalization.

### [153] [The First Token Knows: Single-Decode Confidence for Hallucination Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05166)
*Mina Gabriel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过只需单次解码的首标记置信度（phi_first）来检测语言模型在问答任务中的幻觉（错误或虚假的生成），在无需多次采样的情况下，表现优于或等同于原有的自一致性和语义自一致性方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的自一致性方法检测幻觉需多次生成答案并比对一致性，操作复杂且受词汇变化影响大；语义自一致性虽用语义聚类提高了鲁棒性，但带来高计算、外部推理成本。作者希望找到一种低成本、无需多次采样的新方法。

Method: 本文提出phi_first方法：在仅一次贪婪解码基础上，利用第一个内容词的Top-K概率归一化熵，作为置信度指标检测幻觉，避免采样和外部推理消耗。通过与标准自一致性及语义自一致性比较，量化其性能。

Result: 在三个7-8B参数的指令微调模型和两个基准集上，phi_first的AUROC均值为0.820，优于语义自一致性的0.793与原自一致性的0.791。与语义一致性指标具有中强相关性，两者结合仅带来微小提升。

Conclusion: 大部分利用多样本一致性捕获的不确定性信息，其实已蕴含在首次token分布中。建议在使用基于采样的不确定性估计前，默认先采用低成本的phi_first指标。

Abstract: Self-consistency detects hallucinations by generating multiple sampled answers to a question and measuring agreement, but this requires repeated decoding and can be sensitive to lexical variation. Semantic self-consistency improves this by clustering sampled answers by meaning using natural language inference, but it adds both sampling cost and external inference overhead. We show that first-token confidence, phi_first, computed from the normalized entropy of the top-K logits at the first content-bearing answer token of a single greedy decode, matches or modestly exceeds semantic self-consistency on closed-book short-answer factual question answering. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models and two benchmarks, phi_first achieves a mean AUROC of 0.820, compared with 0.793 for semantic agreement and 0.791 for standard surface-form self-consistency. A subsumption test shows that phi_first is moderately to strongly correlated with semantic agreement, and combining the two signals yields only a small AUROC improvement over phi_first alone. These results suggest that much of the uncertainty information captured by multi-sample agreement is already available in the model's initial token distribution. We argue that phi_first should be reported as a default low-cost baseline before invoking sampling-based uncertainty estimation.

</details>


### [154] [Implicit Representations of Grammaticality in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05197)
*Yingshan Susan Wang,Linlu Qiu,Zhaofeng Wu,Roger P. Levy,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文探讨了大型语言模型（LMs）内部是否学到了与字符串概率无关的语法性知识，通过对内部表示做线性探针，发现LM内部某种程度隐含有语法性辨别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型通过最大化语料库似然被训练出来，虽然在某些受控环境下能区分语法正确与错误句子，但整体上用概率区分语法性表现不突出。因此作者想探究LM的内部是否隐含了超越概率之外的语法知识。

Method: 作者通过对自然文本集扰动构造语法错误的句子，生成包含语法正确/不正确数据集。在此基础上，在LM内部表示（隐藏层）上训练一个简单线性探针，评估其对语法性的判别能力，并将其与传统的概率判断进行比较，还测试了其语义合理性辨别与跨语言的泛化能力。

Result: 线性探针在语法性判别的基准测试上优于基于概率的方法，对人类语法性判断的基准也能很好泛化。对语义合理性的判别则不如概率方法。探针还在多种语言上展现出一定跨语种泛化能力。此外，探针分数与字符串概率相关性较低，说明LM内部表示确实隐含了概率以外的语法信息。

Conclusion: LM的隐藏层内部表示在一定程度上学会了独立于输出概率的语法判别能力，表明概率建模之外，语言模型还学到了一定的隐式语法知识，对未来的模型解释性研究具有启示作用。

Abstract: Grammaticality and likelihood are distinct notions in human language. Pretrained language models (LMs), which are probabilistic models of language fitted to maximize corpus likelihood, generate grammatically well-formed text and discriminate well between grammatical and ungrammatical sentences in tightly controlled minimal pairs. However, their string probabilities do not sharply discriminate between grammatical and ungrammatical sentences overall. But do LMs implicitly acquire a grammaticality distinction distinct from string probability? We explore this question through studying internal representations of LMs, by training a linear probe on a dataset of grammatical and (synthetic) ungrammatical sentences obtained by applying perturbations to a naturalistic text corpus. We find that this simple grammaticality probe generalizes to human-curated grammaticality judgment benchmarks and outperforms LM probability-based grammaticality judgments. When applied to semantic plausibility benchmarks, in which both members of a minimal pair are grammatical and differ in only plausibility, the probe however performs worse than string probability. The English-trained probe also exhibits nontrivial cross-lingual generalization, outperforming string probabilities on grammaticality benchmarks in numerous other languages. Additionally, probe scores correlate only weakly with string probabilities. These results collectively suggest that LMs acquire to some extent an implicit grammaticality distinction within their hidden layers.

</details>

### [155] [From Language to Logic: A Theoretical Architecture for VLM-Grounded Safe Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04327)
*Kristy Sakano,Kalonji Harrington,Mumu Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将人类提供的安全规则和语义偏好集成到户外自主机器人导航中的架构，将自然语言规则转化为信号时序逻辑（STL）规范，结合视觉-语言模型实现零样本场景理解，以提升机器人在非结构化环境下的安全与自主性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人在非结构化户外环境中的自主导航尚难有效结合高层次的人类安全规则和语义偏好，尤其是在实时动态场景下。缺乏人在环路的灵活性和智能理解，导致安全性与操作性受限。需要一种能够人机协作、动态响应且可解释的导航决策机制。

Method: 采用一种新架构，将人类自然语言中的安全规则与操作员语义偏好转化为STL规范。其中，基于环境的规则编码进2D代价地图，时序动态要求则通过STL在运行时监控。假设利用视觉-语言模型实现零样本理解，建立人类指令、语义特征与环境限制间的映射。

Result: 建立了原型导航模型，能在满足STL规范和操作员软偏好的前提下实现形式化的导航决策和环境属性监控。实验表明该方法可将人类安全规则和语义理解有效应用于机器人导航，提高自主性和场景适应性。

Conclusion: 该架构实现了自然语言规则到机器人实际行动的无缝转换，提升了机器人在复杂环境下的安全性和人类理解能力。验证了用VLM及STL规范辅以运行时监控能大幅增强自主导航系统的灵活性和可信度。

Abstract: We propose an architecture for integrating high-level, human-provided safety rules and operator-aligned semantic preferences into autonomous robot navigation in unstructured outdoor environments. In our approach, natural-language rules are translated into Signal Temporal Logic (STL) specifications that guide planning and navigation during runtime. Persistent, environment-centric rules and terrain preferences are grounded into a 2D cost map, while temporally dynamic requirements are expressed as STL specifications to be monitored during runtime. We hypothesize the use of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for zero-shot scene understanding, enabling mapping between human instructions, semantic features, and environmental constraints. Within this framework, we construct an illustrative navigation model that is designed to satisfy a set of STL-encoded specifications and soft operator preferences through formal satisfaction metrics embedded into environmental properties and runtime monitoring.

### [157] [Autonomous Laparoscope Control through Unified Mechanics-Based Representation of Multimodal Intraoperative Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04408)
*Xiaojian Li,Jin Fang,Yudong Shi,Xilin Xiao,Kai Yan,Kang Min,Ling Li,Hua Tang,Hangjie Mo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于多模态信号统一力学建模的腔镜持镜机器人控制方法，实现了在保证RCM约束和降低穿刺口负载的同时，支持柔顺操作和自主目标追踪，并通过仿真和动物实验验证了多任务能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有腔镜持镜机器人难以有效融合位置、力/力矩、图像等多种手术信息，导致视野控制不理想，影响手术安全性和操作效率。因此需要一种统一、协调融合多模态信号的方法，实现更智能、稳定的腔镜控制。

Method: 作者设计了多信息源的映射策略，将位置、力/力矩、图像等信号统一为操作空间中的等效“力矩（wrench）”表示。采用任务优先策略，将不同任务对应的力矩分别注入任务空间和零空间，并通过优先级投影合成最终控制指令。以RCM位置、力/力矩传感器和内窥镜图像为例，分别构建了用于RCM约束、柔顺操作和视觉跟踪的wrench。

Result: 在手术模型和活体猪实验中，方案能够同时支持柔顺持镜操作和自主视觉跟踪，并有效保持RCM几何约束，减少了穿刺口的持续受力，验证了多任务、多模态任务并行能力。

Conclusion: 本文方法实现了多模态手术信息的统一机制力学建模，能够在保证手术关键约束的同时，提升腔镜机器人多任务控制能力，有助于推动智能手术机器人系统的发展。

Abstract: Laparoscope-holding robots can provide surgeons with a stable laparoscopic field of view (FOV) and reduce the burden on human assistants. To maintain an ideal intraoperative FOV, the robot must continuously adjust the laparoscope pose according to intraoperative information. However, intraoperative multimodal signals, such as position, force/torque, and images, differ markedly in physical meaning and units, making it difficult to build a unified representation and to generate control commands that can be used directly for laparoscope control. To address this issue, we propose a laparoscope-holding robot control method based on unified mechanics modeling of multimodal information. First, we design mapping strategies for multiple intraoperative sources, including position, force/torque, and images, and unify them into an equivalent-wrench representation in the operational space. Then, using a task-priority scheme, we inject the wrenches into the task space and the null space, respectively, and synthesize laparoscope control commands via task-priority projection, thereby achieving consistent representation and coordinated fusion of multimodal information within a single framework. Finally, taking the intraoperative remote center of motion (RCM) position, force/torque sensor readings, and laparoscopic images as examples, we construct an RCM-constraint wrench to enforce the RCM geometric constraint and reduce the contact force at the trocar site, a laparoscope-manipulation wrench to enable compliant dragging, and an instrument-tracking wrench to achieve autonomous visual tracking of the instruments. Experiments on a surgical phantom and in vivo porcine trials demonstrate that the proposed method supports multi-task operation, including compliant laparoscope manipulation and autonomous instrument tracking, while maintaining the RCM constraint and reducing sustained trocar-site loading.

</details>


### [158] [Tightly-Coupled Estimation and Guidance for Robust Low-Thrust Rendezvous via Adaptive Homotopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04481)
*Batu Candan,Simone Servadio*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于最小燃料低推力交会的自适应鲁棒制导方法，实现了导航信心与控制平滑性的实时耦合，大幅度提高了在感知退化等异常情况下的制导精度和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的bang-bang最优控制方法对误差估计和传感器异常高度敏感，导致在非合作目标交会场景下易出现失控，因此迫切需要提升制导的安全性和鲁棒性。

Method: 方法采用Clohessy-Wiltshire坐标系建模相对运动，利用带多重调谐因子（MTF）的线性卡尔曼滤波对平移状态滤波和不可信测量方向进行抑制。导航状态置信分数实时映射到间接最优控制的同伦理参数，实现制导策略从激进bang-bang到平滑保守的自适应切换。

Result: 数值仿真显示，固定bang-bang策略和传统滤波下控制器终端误差很大；而所提的MTF自适应同伦理控制器能将误差从百米级降至亚米级，控制消耗仅略高于理论最优值。MTF机制进一步提升了精度和效率。

Conclusion: 自适应同伦理是核心鲁棒机制，MTF协同有效提升制导性能。该在线方法实现快速、可靠求解，展现了实际工程应用潜力。

Abstract: Minimum-fuel low-thrust rendezvous guidance yields bang-bang control structures highly sensitive to estimation errors, sensor anomalies, and solver regularization, making aggressive closed-loop execution brittle for uncooperative proximity operations. This paper proposes a tightly-coupled estimation and guidance architecture where navigation confidence directly modulates the homotopy parameter of a receding-horizon indirect optimal control solver. Relative motion is modeled in the Clohessy-Wiltshire frame. The translational state is estimated via a linear Kalman filter augmented by a Multiple Tuning Factors (MTF) covariance inflation mechanism that suppresses suspicious innovation directions. A composite score from the normalized innovation and MTF activity is mapped online to the homotopy parameter, allowing the controller to relax toward a smoother, conservative regime when confidence degrades, and recover fuel-efficient bang-bang control as sensing improves. Numerical results under severe measurement degradation show fixed bang-bang guidance remains brittle; both plain-KF and MTF-KF fixed-epsilon controllers yield large terminal miss distances. Conversely, the proposed MTF-adaptive homotopy controller reduces terminal miss by roughly two orders of magnitude, from hundreds of meters to sub-meter levels, requiring only a moderate increase in control effort versus the open-loop fuel-optimal benchmark. A comparison indicates adaptive homotopy is the dominant robustness mechanism, while MTF provides additional accuracy and efficiency improvements. The receding-horizon implementation exhibits consistently fast and reliable solution times, supporting the practical online viability of the proposed method.

</details>


### [159] [HDFlow: Hierarchical Diffusion-Flow Planning for Long-horizon Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04525)
*Nandiraju Gireesh,Yuanliang Ju,Chaoyi Xu,Weiheng Liu,Yuxuan Wan,He Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: HDFlow 提出了一种结合扩散模型和流模型的分层生成式路径规划框架，兼顾了探索力与实时性，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式模型在长时序、稀疏奖励任务上表现突出，但缺乏清晰的分层规划结构，且计算上难以满足实时性要求（如扩散模型须迭代去噪）。本文旨在设计兼具分层能力与高效执行的规划框架。

Method: 提出HDFlow分层框架：利用高层的扩散规划器在潜在空间生成具有战略意义的子目标，增强探索性；低层则由Rectified Flow流模型根据子目标高效生成平滑、密集的运动轨迹，利用流模型ODE推理的高效性。

Conclusion: HDFlow 实现了有效的分层生成式规划，兼顾战略性探索与底层高效轨迹生成，为长时序复杂任务提供了优越解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in generative models have shown promise in generating behavior plans for long-horizon, sparse reward tasks. While these approaches have achieved promising results, they often lack a principled framework for hierarchical decomposition and struggle with the computational demands of real-time execution, due to their iterative denoising process. In this work, we introduce Hierarchical Diffusion-Flow (HDFlow), a novel hierarchical planning framework that optimally leverages the strengths of diffusion and rectified flow models to overcome the limitations of single-paradigm generative planners. HDFlow employs a high-level diffusion planner to generate sequences of strategic subgoals in a learned latent space, capitalizing on diffusion's powerful exploratory capabilities. These subgoals then guide a low-level rectified flow planner that generates smooth and dense trajectories, exploiting the speed and efficiency of ordinary differential equation (ODE)-based trajectory generation. We evaluate HDFlow on four challenging furniture assembly tasks in both simulation and real-world, where it significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Furthermore, we also showcase our method's generalizability on two long-horizon benchmarks comprising diverse locomotion and manipulation tasks. Project website: https://hdflow-page.github.io/

Abstract: The representativeness of synthetic pre-crash scenarios is crucial for assessing the safety impact of Driving Automation Systems through virtual simulations. Conventional significance testing is inadequate, as it focuses on detecting differences rather than establishing practical equivalence. This study addresses the research gap by extending our previous work on a Bayesian Region of Practical Equivalence (ROPE)-based equivalence testing framework by introducing a binning-based approach to define appropriate statistics and equivalence criteria. Two binning-based statistics are proposed to measure practically meaningful distributional differences between datasets in the context of safety impact assessment. The framework's applicability is demonstrated through a case study, which tests the practical equivalence of two synthetic rear-end pre-crash datasets with a previously developed reference dataset in the context of the safety impact assessment of an Automatic Emergency Braking system. The results show that the framework provides informative quantitative assessments of practical equivalence as well as diagnostic insights into the divergence of datasets. Although the demonstration focuses on rear-end pre-crash scenarios, the framework is generic and extensible to broader validation contexts, providing an interpretable and principled basis for practical equivalence assessment across diverse synthetic data applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人交接物体（handover）的方法多为被动感知，难以应对不同物体和人类行为的多样性，特别是在区分牢固抓握与偶然接触时存在挑战。

Method: 提出主动感知策略：机器人主动施加探索性动作，感知人类施加的力，并利用贝叶斯线性模型对接触状态进行建模，通过多方向的受力区分抓握与触碰，实现信息主动获取。

Abstract: Robot-to-human object handover is an essential skill for robot assistants, from serving drinks at home to passing surgical tools in the operating room. We expect robots to perform handover robustly -- to release the object only after a firm human grasp while ignoring incidental touches. Existing passive-sensing methods struggle to generalize across diverse objects and human behaviors, as they lack informative perturbations to disambiguate different contact conditions, such as firm grasp versus incidental touch. We propose an active sensing approach for robust handovers: the robot applies information-gathering motions and senses the resulting human-applied forces to infer the contact state. A firm grasp produces forces in multiple directions, while an accidental touch does not. To capture this distinction, we model the contact state with a Bayesian linear model: a distribution over piecewise-linear mappings from robot motions to human-applied forces. This model enables firm grasp detection and active information gathering. In experiments with 12 participants and 30 diverse rigid objects, our method achieved a 97.5% success rate -- over 30% higher than two common baselines.

*Huimin Wang,Yue Wang,Bihao Cui,Pengxiang Li,Ben Lu,Mingqian Wang,Tong Wang,Chuan Tang,Teng Zhang,Kun Zhan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动驾驶决策与规划面临高效性、可解释性和在线调整（编辑）难题。以往方法多需额外的后处理网络且编辑能力有限。

Method: ReflectDrive-2将轨迹表示为离散token，通过掩码并行扩散解码实现规划；其独特之处在于模型自身承担AutoEdit——对轨迹token实现原地修订，无需额外网络。训练分两阶段：先用结构感知扰动训练模型复原expert轨迹，再进行全流程强化学习微调（reward回传给最终编辑后的轨迹，端到端优化）。同时设计高效的推理解码堆栈，加速部署。

Result: 在模拟环境NAVSIM上，ReflectDrive-2仅用摄像头输入获得91.0 PDMS，best-of-6 oracle设定下达94.8 PDMS，并可实时运行（31.8ms延迟/NVIDIA Thor）。使用强化学习后，AutoEdit的推理性能提升显著（PDMS提升1.9，明显优于仅监督学习）。

Abstract: We introduce ReflectDrive-2, a masked discrete diffusion planner with separate action expert for autonomous driving that represents plans as discrete trajectory tokens and generates them through parallel masked decoding. This discrete token space enables in-place trajectory revision: AutoEdit rewrites selected tokens using the same model, without requiring an auxiliary refinement network. To train this capability, we use a two-stage procedure. First, we construct structure-aware perturbations of expert trajectories along longitudinal progress and lateral heading directions and supervise the model to recover the original expert trajectory. We then fine-tune the full decision--draft--reflect rollout with reinforcement learning (RL), assigning terminal driving reward to the final post-edit trajectory and propagating policy-gradient credit through full-rollout transitions. Full-rollout RL proves crucial for coupling drafting and editing: under supervised training alone, inference-time AutoEdit improves PDMS by at most $0.3$, whereas RL increases its gain to $1.9$. We also co-design an efficient reflective decoding stack for the decision--draft--reflect pipeline, combining shared-prefix KV reuse, Alternating Step Decode, and fused on-device unmasking. On NAVSIM, ReflectDrive-2 achieves $91.0$ PDMS with camera-only input and $94.8$ PDMS in a best-of-6 oracle setting, while running at $31.8$ ms average latency on NVIDIA Thor.

In the second stage, RL executes the insertion and enables recovery from failures during contact-rich interactions. To better exploit tactile feedback, we introduce tactile group sampling to increase coverage of critical contact segments during training, and design a tactile critic to more accurately evaluate policy values, improving insertion performance while maintaining low contact forces. Elastic bands routed through printed hooks store energy that folds the sheet into programmed 3D geometries, while the flat state allows accurate placement of electronics and magnets before deployment. The same substrate doubles as electrodes for capacitive touch and supports a reusable platform I/O palette with Hall sensors and eccentric rotating mass (ERM) motors for docking detection and vibration actuation. We also derive a closed-form folding model that balances hinge stiffness with elastic band moment to predict equilibrium fold angles; experiments validate the model and yield a design map linking hinge thickness, band size, and hook spacing to target angles. Using this workflow we realize multiple polyhedral modules and demonstrate three applications: a cube that highlights the potential of self-folding for scalable modular robot collectives, a deployable gripper, and a tendon-driven finger. The method is low cost, stimulus-free, and integrates actuation and sensing.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行为克隆虽然易用，但无法自我改进，且现有离线-到在线的方法常因数据分布不匹配，导致策略劣化。

Method: Q2RL包括两个核心步骤：（1）通过少量环境交互从行为克隆策略中提取Q函数（Q-Estimation）；（2）基于Q值在行为克隆和强化学习策略之间切换（Q-Gating），用于收集数据并指导RL策略训练。

Result: 在D4RL和robomimic等基准的操作任务中，Q2RL在成功率和收敛速度显著优于现有方法，可在高度复杂的操控任务中1-2小时在线训练下取得最高100%的成功率，并较原始BC提升多达3.75倍。

Existing offline-to-online learning methods often cause policies to replace previously learned good actions due to a distribution mismatch between offline data and online learning. In this work, we propose Q2RL, Q-Estimation and Q-Gating from BC for Reinforcement Learning, an algorithm for efficient offline-to-online learning. Our method consists of two parts: (1) Q-Estimation extracts a Q-function from a BC policy using a few interaction steps with the environment, followed by online RL with (2) Q-Gating, which switches between BC and RL policy actions based on their respective Q-values to collect samples for RL policy training. Across manipulation tasks from D4RL and robomimic benchmarks, Q2RL outperforms SOTA offline-to-online learning baselines on success rate and time to convergence. Q2RL is efficient enough to be applied in an on-robot RL setting, learning robust policies for contact-rich and high precision manipulation tasks such as pipe assembly and kitting, in 1-2 hours of online interaction, achieving success rates of up to 100% and up to 3.75x improvement against the original BC policy. ### [176] [A Closed-Form Dual-Barrier CBF Safety Filter for Holonomic Robots on Incrementally Built Occupancy Grid Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05182)
*Himanshu Paudel,Basanta Joshi,Dhirendra Raj Madai,Alina Bartaula,Biman Rimal,Sanjay Neupane*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于全向移动机器人在占据网格图中进行增量探索时的基于双障碍控制障碍函数（CBF）的实时安全过滤器，有效实现了在未知和已知障碍物之间的安全速度控制，并在实际硬件飞行验证中实现零碰撞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人探索未知环境时，尚未探索的区域带来不可避免的碰撞风险，尤其当前置传感器无法感知这些区域的障碍物时更为严重。现有方法难以在资源受限、需要实时反应的场景下兼顾探索效率和安全性，因此需要一种计算开销低且保障安全的控制方法。

Method: 作者提出了一种双障碍CBF安全过滤器，通过从占据网格的有符号距离场中解析推导出两个约束：一是避免已映射障碍物，二是限制进入未探索区域。该方法可以在每个控制周期仅通过求解一个小型线性系统实现，适合计算资源有限的平台，并在速度空间作为最小侵入式补偿，能够与任意控制器（甚至学习型方法）结合。另外，采用自适应增益机制调节对未知区域的约束强度，提升探索效率。

Result: 该方法在硬件平台（如PX4四旋翼）上的室内飞行实验中，所有测试均实现零碰撞，验证了其实时性、低开销和高安全性。

Conclusion: 提出的双障碍CBF安全过滤器能在资源受限、实时性要求高的环境下，确保机器人高效且安全地进行未知环境探索，对前沿传感器配备的机器人具有良好适用性和推广价值。

Abstract: We present a dual-barrier control barrier function (CBF) safety filter for real-time, safety-critical velocity control of holonomic robots operating in incrementally built occupancy grid maps. As a robot explores an unknown environment, unmapped regions introduce irreducible uncertainty, since obstacle geometry beyond the explored frontier is unknown, making entry into such regions a source of collision risk, especially with front-facing sensors. To address this, we enforce two constraints: avoidance of mapped obstacles and restriction from unexplored regions. Both constraints are derived analytically from the occupancy grid's signed distance field, yielding a closed-form safety filter that requires only a small linear system solve per cycle. On resource-constrained platforms such as the Raspberry Pi, where SLAM and planning already consume significant compute, the low overhead of the proposed filter preserves resources. An adaptive gain schedule relaxes the frontier constraint in information-rich regions and tightens it in well-mapped areas, improving exploration efficiency while maintaining safety. The filter operates in velocity space as a minimally invasive correction and composes with arbitrary nominal controllers, including learning-based methods. Hardware flight experiments on a PX4-controlled quadrotor demonstrate zero collisions across multiple indoor runs.

</details>
